Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-08-02 Hans de Goede <hdegoede at redhat dot com> - 2.3.7-24 - Stop using the obsolete pthread_mutexattr_setkind_np function (really fix FTBFS and runtime issues in dependend packages)
2021-08-02 Hans de Goede <hdegoede at redhat dot com> - 2.3.7-23 - Fix libclan23Core not being linked against libpthread which is causing FTBFS issues in other packages
2021-07-21 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 2.3.7-22 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_35_Mass_Rebuild
2021-01-25 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 2.3.7-21 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 2.3.7-20 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 2.3.7-19 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
